//JS Cookie

/*!
 highlight v4
 Highlights arbitrary terms.
 &lt;http://johannburkard.de/blog/programming/javascript/highlight-javascript-text-higlighting-jquery-plugin.html&gt;

 Johann Burkard

(function($){$.fn.highlight=function(pat){function innerHighlight(node,pat){var skip=0;if(node.nodeType==3){var pos=node.data.toUpperCase().indexOf(pat);if(pos&gt;=0){var spannode=document.createElement("span");spannode.className="highlight";var middlebit=node.splitText(pos);var endbit=middlebit.splitText(pat.length);var middleclone=middlebit.cloneNode(true);spannode.appendChild(middleclone);middlebit.parentNode.replaceChild(spannode,middlebit);skip=1}}else{if(node.nodeType==1&amp;&amp;node.childNodes&amp;&amp;!/(script|style)/i.test(node.tagName)){for(var i=0;i&lt;node.childNodes.length;++i){i+=innerHighlight(node.childNodes[i],pat)}}}return skip}return this.length&amp;&amp;pat&amp;&amp;pat.length?this.each(function(){innerHighlight(this,pat.toUpperCase())}):this};$.fn.removeHighlight=function(){return this.find("span.highlight").each(function(){this.parentNode.firstChild.nodeName;with(this.parentNode){replaceChild(this.firstChild,this);normalize()}}).end()}})(jQuery);

           <span>
            How to choose the right data storage drive for your computer and popular storage options available in market?
           </span>
          </div>

          <div class="date-outer">
           <div class="date-posts">
            <div class="post-outer">
             <article class="post hentry" id="6359499979492538226" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
              <h1 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name headline">
               <a href="http://www.technovisitors.com/2013/12/How-to-choose-right-data-storage-and-available-options.html" itemprop="url">
                How to choose the right data storage drive for your computer and popular storage options available in market?
               </a>
              </h1>
              <div class="topmeta">
               <div class="pull-right inner">
                <a class="zoom-text zoom-in-text" href="#A+">
                 A
                 <span>
                  +
                 </span>
                </a>
                <a class="zoom-text zoom-out-text" href="#A-">
                 A
                 <span>
                  -
                 </span>
                </a>
                <div>
                 <div class="addthis_toolbox addthis_default_style addthis_16x16_style">
                  <a class="addthis_button_print">
                   Print
                  </a>
                  <a class="addthis_button_email">
                   Email
                  </a>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div>
                 <form action="javascript:;" class="text-finder" id="text-finder">
                  <input placeholder="Find..." type="text"/>
                  <input type="reset" value=""/>
                 </form>
                </div>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-6359499979492538226" itemprop="description articleBody">
               <div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
                <div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <span style="color: #c00000; line-height: 200%;">
                  <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                   Are you looking for your
most suitable data storage? For this, you would require to get answers to few questions
like - What important features one should consider when selecting a storage
device? What are the main types of storage and what most popular local data
storage devices available to purchase in market? And what are the pros and cons
of these storage devices.
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
                 <tbody>
                  <tr>
                   <td style="text-align: center;">
                    <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-lpMi7_YT-ng/Uq6Rie6YomI/AAAAAAAAAEM/33PhOxSuDvo/s1600/Storage+drives.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                     <img alt="Large number of storage disk drives are available to purhcase in market" border="0" height="400" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-lpMi7_YT-ng/Uq6Rie6YomI/AAAAAAAAAEM/33PhOxSuDvo/s400/Storage+drives.JPG" title="Large number of storage disk drives are available to purhcase in market" width="377"/>
                    </a>
                   </td>
                  </tr>
                  <tr>
                   <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                    <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                     Different storage drive options available for buyers in market
                    </span>
                   </td>
                  </tr>
                 </tbody>
                </table>
                <h2 style="text-align: left;">
                 <span style="background-color: #cfe2f3; font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; font-weight: normal; line-height: 200%;">
                  <span style="color: blue;">
                   How to choose the right data storage drive for your computer?
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </h2>
                <div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 200%;">
                  Depending on type of work or
businesses, the requirement type of data storage media usually vary from one
user to other. Today, from very small sized USB pen drive to the large cloud
options available for customers. You can choose your best storage disk option
according to your requirement.
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  In my earlier post I discussed about
                 </span>
                 <span style="background-color: white; color: blue; font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 18px;">
                  <a href="http://www.technovisitors.com/2013/12/How-to-asses-right-sized-hard-disk-storage.html" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 18px;" target="_blank">
                   <span style="color: blue;">
                    how to determine the size of your hard drive storage device
                   </span>
                  </a>
                 </span>
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 200%;">
                  , and hope in this post you will find your most suitable storage disk option.
                 </span>
                </div>
                <h3 style="text-align: left;">
                 <span style="background-color: #d9d2e9; font-weight: normal; line-height: 200%;">
                  <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                   What features
you should check while choosing new data storage drive?
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </h3>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <!--[if !supportLists]-->
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <b>
                    1.
                    <span style="line-height: normal;">
                    </span>
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <b>
                    Compatibility
with your system:
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   Check
for the compatibility of selected storage device with your system, and it is must
for Mac or Linux users.
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <!--[if !supportLists]-->
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <span style="font-weight: bold; line-height: 200%;">
                   2.
                   <span style="line-height: normal;">
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <b>
                    Automatic
backup:
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   This feature offers great
reliability. It is all about keeping multiple copies of data to recover from
accidental deletion.
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <!--[if !supportLists]-->
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <span style="font-weight: bold; line-height: 200%;">
                   3.
                   <span style="line-height: normal;">
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <b>
                    Shock
protection:
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <b>
                   </b>
                   The
shock proof features should be highly expected for the portable hard drives.
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <!--[if !supportLists]-->
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <span style="font-weight: bold; line-height: 200%;">
                   4.
                   <span style="line-height: normal;">
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <b>
                    USB
support:
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <b>
                   </b>
                   The USB 2.0 and USB 3.0
connection support is standard, nowadays. Today, large number of devices required
to have USB port on computer to get connected with. USB 3.0 is three times
faster and offers very quick copying of data.
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <!--[if !supportLists]-->
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <span style="font-weight: bold; line-height: 200%;">
                   5.
                   <span style="line-height: normal;">
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <b>
                    Password
protection:
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <b>
                   </b>
                   The
users carrying sensitive data on their storage mediums must opt for password protection
feature storage. You should also read
                  </span>
                 </span>
                 <span style="line-height: 18px; text-indent: 0px;">
                  <a href="http://technovisitors.blogspot.in/2013/03/myidkey-password-protection-with.html" target="_blank">
                   <span style="background-color: white; color: blue; font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                    myIDkey - the safest Passwords protection USB device
                   </span>
                  </a>
                  <span style="font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;">
                   .
                  </span>
                 </span>
                 <br/>
                 <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin: 12pt 0in 0.25in 0.5in; text-indent: 0px;">
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <!--[if !supportLists]-->
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <span style="font-weight: bold; line-height: 200%;">
                   6.
                   <span style="line-height: normal;">
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <b>
                    Surf
online for best deal:
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <b>
                   </b>
                   You
must surf online stores before buying a storage device to get a best deal.
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <h3 style="text-align: left;">
                 <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                  <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                   <span style="background-color: #d9d2e9; font-weight: normal;">
                    What are
the main types of data storage options?
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </h3>
                <div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .25in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                  <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                   There are two types of
storage options available for users to store their data. Depending on your
requirement you can choose any of these two:
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo2; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <!--[if !supportLists]-->
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   a)
                   <span style="line-height: normal;">
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   Local storage
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo2; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <!--[if !supportLists]-->
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   b)
                   <span style="line-height: normal;">
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   Remote storage
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .25in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                  <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                   In local storage, you have
option for choosing any physically accessed storage like USB and hard drive,
while the remote storage includes cloud based options.
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <h3 style="text-align: left;">
                 <span style="background-color: #d9d2e9; font-weight: normal; line-height: 200%;">
                  <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                   What are
the most popular local data storage drives available in market?
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </h3>
                <h3 style="text-align: left;">
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; font-weight: normal;">
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   1.
                   <span style="line-height: normal;">
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: #ead1dc; line-height: 200%;">
                   USB
Pen drive
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </h3>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                  <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                   It is considered to be the best portable option for every user because
it is smaller in size and can easily be fitted inside your key chain, ear top,
writing pen and even in a small rings. The USB sticks available in different
storage options from 1GB to 128 GB capacity. Nowadays, the USB making companies
have started enveloping USB drives with steel, which makes them sturdier.
                   <b>
                    <o:p>
                    </o:p>
                   </b>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                 <br/>
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 200%;">
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <b>
                    Advantages of USB pen
drives:
                   </b>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 200%;">
                  <b>
                  </b>
                  Highly portable, easier
to use and having sturdy built-up.
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <b>
                    Disadvantages:
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <b>
                   </b>
                   USBs with high storage are
relatively expensive in compare to other options, Risky for picking up viruses
and spreading from one computer to other.
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <h3 style="text-align: left;">
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <span style="font-weight: normal; line-height: 200%;">
                   2.
                   <span style="line-height: normal;">
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <span style="background-color: #ead1dc; font-weight: normal;">
                    External hard disk drives
                   </span>
                   <b>
                    <o:p>
                    </o:p>
                   </b>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </h3>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                  <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                   The external hard drive is also quite similar to computer drive but
it differs in having plug in and out capabilities to your computer. There are
two sizes of hard disks available in market  first 3.5-inch (8.9cm) called
desktop external hard drive and the other 2.5 inch (6.4cm) that is known as
portable external hard drive.
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                  <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                   Both the storage hard drives can store 500GB to 4TB data and your
can connect them to your computer via a USB cable. The portable hard disk
storage is light-weight device with much larger storage space than USB sticks. It
comes in between 250GB to 1.5TB of storage space.
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                  <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                   On the other hand, an external hard drive being much bigger than
portable one is best suitable for using as an additional hard drive.
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <b>
                    Advantages of external
hard disk:
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   Large
storage and easily portable.
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <b>
                    Disadvantages:
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   Required additional care while
handling as it can damage with just drop or during electrical surges.
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <h3 style="text-align: left;">
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <span style="background-color: #f3f3f3; font-weight: normal; line-height: 200%;">
                   3.
                   <span style="line-height: normal;">
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <span style="background-color: #ead1dc; font-weight: normal;">
                    SSD (Solid State Drives)
                   </span>
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </h3>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                  <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                   Unlike other traditional magnetic drives, a SSD drive does not
consists of rotating platters, hence it is more robust. Besides this, for not
having any moving part, it is less power hungry. Being robust and low power consuming,
SSDs are most suitable for potable tablets and laptops. The SSDs are best
choice for the users, who require very fast read, write performance and
robustness. It is mostly available in 64 to 256GB storage capacity.
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <b>
                    Advantages of SSD storage:
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   Faster, reliable and
robust
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <b>
                    Disadvantages:
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <b>
                   </b>
                   Comparatively much expensive
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <h3 style="text-align: left;">
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <span style="font-weight: normal; line-height: 200%;">
                   4.
                   <span style="line-height: normal;">
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <span style="background-color: #ead1dc; font-weight: normal;">
                    DVD (Digital Versatile Drives)
                   </span>
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </h3>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                  <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                   A DVD can store data between 4.7GB and 17.08GB. You can store your
favorite movies, songs and software on a DVD.
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                 <span style="line-height: 115%;">
                  <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                   The
                  </span>
                  <a href="http://www.technovisitors.com/2013/02/blu-ray-hot-technology-you-should-know.html" target="_blank">
                   <span style="background-color: white; color: blue; font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                    latest Blue ray disc technology is the better and advanced variant of DVDs
                   </span>
                  </a>
                 </span>
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; line-height: 115%;">
                  . It is much faster and having
more storage space than CD and DVDs.
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <b>
                    Advantages of DVDs
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <b>
                    :
                   </b>
                   Inexpensive and easily portable
in packs.
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <b>
                    Disadvantages:
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <b>
                   </b>
                   Have short life span, not as
reliable as other storage devices.
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <h3 style="text-align: left;">
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <span style="font-weight: normal; line-height: 200%;">
                   5.
                   <span style="line-height: normal;">
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <span style="background-color: #ead1dc; font-weight: normal;">
                    NAS (Network Attached Storage)
                   </span>
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </h3>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                  <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                   In compare to other disks, the expensive network attached storage
drives consists of several connected hard drives hence, can store a large
volume of information (data). Since these drives facilitate wireless sharing,
so perfectly useful for individual families or small businesses. Such
networking hard drives allow many users simultaneous access and it works
through routers or Wi-Fi.
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <b>
                    Advantages of NAS:
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   The automatic scheduled backup
saves the contents wirelessly even if a user forgets about it. Through NAS, you
can also stream required contents to your TV, computer or mobile devices.
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <b>
                    Disadvantages:
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   Being available on network, the
NAS storage devices has to be remained on for 24 hours as a user may require
data access, anytime.
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <h3 style="text-align: left;">
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <span style="font-weight: normal; line-height: 200%;">
                   6.
                   <span style="line-height: normal;">
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                   <span style="background-color: #ead1dc; font-weight: normal;">
                    Multimedia hard drives
                   </span>
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </h3>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                  <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                   Multimedia hard drive allows a user watching movies or pictures in
HD format on his TV. Such type of hard drives can store 1 to 2 TB of data. The cheaper
options of multimedia hard drives come without built-in storage and can be
connected to hard drive for sending contents to television. In short, such
storage drives are perfectly suitable for the users who like carrying their multimedia
contents with them.
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="line-height: 200%; margin-bottom: .25in; margin-left: .5in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-justify: inter-ideograph;">
                 <span style="line-height: 200%;">
                  <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                   Hope you would find above information useful. If so, share it with your friends also and add us your circle to remain updated with our upcoming posts.
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
               </div>
               <div style="clear: both;">
               </div>
              </div>
